We were left stranded for the second time in as many days due to train cancellations. As we were on the way out of Xian we wanted to find a hotel near the train station so that it would be easy the next day. We thought that we could not go wrong with the IntercCon and our expectations were well met in all aspects. Arrival and check in was smooth, a welcome drink was much appreciated and so we settled in the Lobby Lounge to compose ourselves after a hot and hectic afternoon spend at the railway station. We decided  to reward ourselves with a nice dinner at Char and that felt like heaven. The very nice atmosphere was accompanied by great food and we were lucky to have met Pierre who provided delightful service. So thanks to InterCon and The Team; in particular Pierre, an otherwise not exactly great day, was saved in the end. We enjoyed a great breakfast next morning and finally went on our way.  Thank you team InterCon and you certainly have our recommendation!

health:

breakfast:

Although I have not experienced most of the InterContinentals in China, but from the recent stays in Hefei, Dalian, and Xi'an (representing the northern, central, and western regions), Xi'an InterContinental is worthy of the title of benchmark!
First of all, let‚Äôs talk about two details: first, the luggage. When checking in, the staff took the luggage out of the car and sent it to the room; The second is takeaway. In the hotels that have been better in recent years, it may be the only one that has staff delivering to the room (at that time, I was picking up takeaway downstairs, and saw the staff deliver the takeaway ordered by other guests from an incubator. .Of course, now many hotels can deliver by robots).
Then catering, hotel catering, especially breakfast, is becoming more and more homogeneous, but each hotel should still have its own local characteristics. Xi‚Äôan InterContinental has done it. Subjectively speaking, the Roujiamo made by the pastry chef even exceeds that of ‚ÄúZiwulu Zhangji‚Äù. (I ordered this Ziwu Road Zhangji when I was hungry. The rating is super high and the taste is great)
As for the hardware, as long as it is not special for a hotel of this standard, it is guaranteed, and there is nothing special to say. However, the Morandi green in the room (feeling as warm as jade), combined with the park outside the window, is still very pleasant.
Regarding location, for travel, there are often some trade-offs between convenience and comfort, but Jingkai Intercontinental basically meets these two points. Downstairs of the hotel is Metro Line 2 and Line 4. It is very convenient to go to the Bell Tower and Datang Everbright City, especially to the North Railway Station. It only takes 13 minutes by taxi, which is really amazing. Of course, if I went to the Terracotta Warriors and Horses, I still chose to stay at holidayinn in Chanba, after all, I have to get up early to catch the time.
